<span id="freeTextContainer8763751058847959621">Spain. A land of eternal passion and unceasing bloodshed. From the vengeance of a pitiless tyrant, four women flee the sacred, once-safe walls of a convent: LUCIA, the proud survivor harboring a murderous secret from the savage clan wars of Sicily...GRACIELLA, the beauty still unpurged of guilt from one reckless, youthful sin...MEGAN, the orphan seeking perilous refuge in</span>
  <span style="display:none" id="freeText8763751058847959621">Spain. A land of eternal passion and unceasing bloodshed. From the vengeance of a pitiless tyrant, four women flee the sacred, once-safe walls of a convent: LUCIA, the proud survivor harboring a murderous secret from the savage clan wars of Sicily...GRACIELLA, the beauty still unpurged of guilt from one reckless, youthful sin...MEGAN, the orphan seeking perilous refuge in the arms of a defiant Basque rebel...and TERESA, the believer haunted by a faith that mocks her with silence. Leaving innocence but not hope behind, they venture into an alien, dazzling world, where each will encounter an unexpected destiny -- and the truth about herself.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer2573213712371199872">“The difference between a rebel and a patriot depends upon who is in power at the moment.” — Sidney Sheldon, Sands of Time<br /><br />The Sands of Time is an action-packed novel published in 1988 by the Master of Unexpected, Sidney Sheldon. <br /><br />The story is set 37 years after the Civil War in Spain or the Spanish Inquisition (which lasted from 1936-1939).   <span style="display:none" id="freeText2573213712371199872">“The difference between a rebel and a patriot depends upon who is in power at the moment.” — Sidney Sheldon, Sands of Time<br /><br />The Sands of Time is an action-packed novel published in 1988 by the Master of Unexpected, Sidney Sheldon. <br /><br />The story is set 37 years after the Civil War in Spain or the Spanish Inquisition (which lasted from 1936-1939). Remember, that Civil War was one of the bloodiest civil wars in history. More than half people lost their homes and lives in the battles for power between the Republicans and the rebel Nationalists in Spain.<br />Going back to the real setting of the story. Dated 1976 in Madrid -Spain, the Spanish government ruled by a authoritarian leader, Leopoldo Martinez had a conflict with the Catholic church. Leopoldo Martinez believes that the church has been hiding and aiding rebels inside their convents. Consequently, he decided to threaten the church which resulted to violence that forced four (4) women to leave the Spanish convent and seek a fight to death against the government.</span>

<div itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope="" itemprop="reviews" class="review" id="review_428801105">
  <link href="http://www.goodreads.com/review/show/428801105" itemprop="url" />
  <a href="/user/show/6375944-saurabh-sharma" class="left imgcol" title="Saurabh Sharma"><img src="http://d.gr-assets.com/users/1451807069p2/6375944.jpg" alt="Saurabh Sharma" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a href="/review/show/428801105?book_show_action=true" itemprop="publishDate" class="reviewDate createdAt right">Oct 11, 2012</a>

      <a href="/user/show/6375944-saurabh-sharma" class="user" title="Saurabh Sharma">Saurabh Sharma</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars"><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="liked it">liked it</span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="liked it"></span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="liked it"></span><span class="staticStar p0" size="15x15" title="liked it"></span><span class="staticStar p0" size="15x15" title="liked it"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText"> · </span>
          <a href="/book/show/11561565-the-sands-of-time" title="Kindle Edition " class="lightGreyText">review of another edition</a>


        


    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span style="" class="readable" id="reviewTextContainer428801105">
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17887807608863048923">Sands of Time by Sydney Sheldon keeps you hooked till the end despite obvious flaws and loopholes in the plot. Based in the backdrop of Spanish Civil war between the Basques and the Spanish government, 'Sands of Time' is a story of Jaime Miro, a legendary, fearless and most-wanted terrorist, fighting for the rights of the Basque people against the authorities. The Spanish Prime Minister is on a hunt for Miro, and has deployed Colonel Acoca to bring Miro to justice for his crimes against the stat</span>
  <span style="display:none" id="freeText17887807608863048923">Sands of Time by Sydney Sheldon keeps you hooked till the end despite obvious flaws and loopholes in the plot. Based in the backdrop of Spanish Civil war between the Basques and the Spanish government, 'Sands of Time' is a story of Jaime Miro, a legendary, fearless and most-wanted terrorist, fighting for the rights of the Basque people against the authorities. The Spanish Prime Minister is on a hunt for Miro, and has deployed Colonel Acoca to bring Miro to justice for his crimes against the state. The story thus becomes a game of chess between Miro and Acoca as both try to out think and outdo each other leading to a number of exciting events. <br /><br />'Sands of Time' opens with a sensational scene at the traditional Bull run festival in Pampalona, where Jaime Miro, hero and freedom fighter to the Basque people is about to carry out a stunning operation to free his mates from the prison cell. This grand scene sets the tone of the novel and is one of the real high points in a story where there are also a few lows. <br /><br />Jaime Miro and his fellow terrorists must leave the country to escape the Spanish Government. However, even as they plan their escape they are joined by 4 nuns, who had fled from the convent when Col. Acoca had raided it in search of the escaped prisoners/terrorists. This leads to a number of interesting situations as the lives of the sisters intermingle with those of the terrorists, and are changed forever. What makes this transformation interesting is the back story of each of the nuns. They all have chequered pasts and the convent for them was a place of solace and shelter from their miserable lives. But, as they are forced back into the real world they must face their demons again. This conflict could have actually made for an interesting sub-plot but sadly the author fails in doing justice to this aspect of the story. As a result it comes across as superfluous and a mere plot device to add erotic and romantic moments to the plot. Though to be honest, one of the nuns actually plays a critical part in the novel, the others more or less serve the aforementioned purpose.<br /><br />There are also a few other situations that just don't seem plausible. There's one in the end concerning Jaime Miro that is simply too far fetched to believe. All these loopholes weaken the story, making it an average story that promised much better things in the beginning. A<br /><br />Although enjoyable to read and gripping at times, the Sands of Time never manages to rise above the average due to its flaws. </span>
  <a onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;" href="#" data-text-id="17887807608863048923">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer7158742137209393109">This is a story of four nuns who were able to escape the hostile military forces of Acoca who got into their convent. They were instructed by the Reverend Mother to take the convent's most precious possession with them and bring it to the next convent where it can be safely kept and where they can seek refuge as well. However, they fall into the hands of the rebel group led by Jaime Miro. <br /><br />Jaime Miro was ultimately the handsomest rebel this story has ever created.   <span style="display:none" id="freeText7158742137209393109">This is a story of four nuns who were able to escape the hostile military forces of Acoca who got into their convent. They were instructed by the Reverend Mother to take the convent's most precious possession with them and bring it to the next convent where it can be safely kept and where they can seek refuge as well. However, they fall into the hands of the rebel group led by Jaime Miro. <br /><br />Jaime Miro was ultimately the handsomest rebel this story has ever created. He was so manly, undeniably charming and witty. The leader of the outlawed Basque guerrilla.<br /><br />On the other hand, each nun had their personal struggles prior to committing themselves in a life of prayer inside the four-walled abode. But,as they faced the real world which they long ago abandoned, each of them has to deal with the secrets of their past while in the hands of the men they eventually fall in love with.<br /><br />With this book, Sheldon once again captivates the readers imagination to make each character vivid and alive. <br /><br /><br /></span>

  <span style="display:none" id="freeText1668023696712416337">It has been an engrossing and entertaining read throughout the time i had this book.The book can be described as a true novel with mixed feelings and emotions throughout and as the title aptly describes, a sequence of events(adventures would be better) and feelings and their change with time.Its worthy of the time you spent<br />A problem i had noticed was that each character had a flashback to him/her and it becomes difficult to match the characters with their flashblack as the story progresses and it doesnt make the kind of impact one would expect from a sheldon creation.I still feel the kind of immorality pictured in the book makes me sick.<br /><br />There has been wonderful situations in the book which creates all kinds of feelings and conflicts in your mind..and it has all the drama and romance required of a novel too.<br /><br />A summary of the story for those who want to read it....<br />Set in spain the story talks of the revolutionary times in spains history where war between the rebels and the government takes place and state of unrest and violence prevails.Four nuns of a <a rel="nofollow" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cistercians">Cistercian</a> convent there finds their fates mixed with those of a group of terrorists(freedon fighters) led by Jaime Mairo and the story is all about their fates in the end.<br /><br /><br /><br /></span>

              <span style="" class="readable" id="reviewTextContainer99137608">
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1224586076700220774">Sidney Sheldon spins a yarn that is both entertaining and addictive. It was a spellbinding moment reading the thick and rich plot. At first, I thought Sands of Times is gory and bloody, chaotic, historical and violent. However, it was the opposite. It was a 400 page full of reminisces of each of the major characters. <br /><br />On the other hand, Sidney Sheldon's writing prowess is sometimes predictable, in a good sense that you want to prove you're right. And when you are, you felt great because you feel</span>
  <span style="display:none" id="freeText1224586076700220774">Sidney Sheldon spins a yarn that is both entertaining and addictive. It was a spellbinding moment reading the thick and rich plot. At first, I thought Sands of Times is gory and bloody, chaotic, historical and violent. However, it was the opposite. It was a 400 page full of reminisces of each of the major characters. <br /><br />On the other hand, Sidney Sheldon's writing prowess is sometimes predictable, in a good sense that you want to prove you're right. And when you are, you felt great because you feel that you are thinking like a poet, a writer, a master.<br /><br />To get you out of boredom or if you want to kill time or to be invigorated from an exhausting activity. Try read a few pages and you'll pay no attention to your watch. Too late for you to notice, you skipped two dinners already, but deep inside you're not empty, instead overflowing with delight for what this story has kept.</span>

<div itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope="" itemprop="reviews" class="review" id="review_168602203">
  <link href="http://www.goodreads.com/review/show/168602203" itemprop="url" />
  <a href="/user/show/5449325-sasha-dayo" class="left imgcol" title="Sasha Dayo"><img src="http://d.gr-assets.com/users/1343468039p2/5449325.jpg" alt="Sasha Dayo" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a href="/review/show/168602203?book_show_action=true" itemprop="publishDate" class="reviewDate createdAt right">May 16, 2011</a>

      <a href="/user/show/5449325-sasha-dayo" class="user" title="Sasha Dayo">Sasha Dayo</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars"><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="it was amazing">it was amazing</span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="it was amazing"></span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="it was amazing"></span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="it was amazing"></span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="it was amazing"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText"> · </span>
          <a href="/book/show/119382.Sands_of_Time" title="Paperback 9780006174431" class="lightGreyText">review of another edition</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span style="" class="readable" id="reviewTextContainer168602203">

<div itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope="" itemprop="reviews" class="review" id="review_1433414491">
  <link href="http://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1433414491" itemprop="url" />
  <a href="/user/show/31780597-rinu-razak" class="left imgcol" title="Rinu Razak"><img src="http://d.gr-assets.com/users/1446650947p2/31780597.jpg" alt="Rinu Razak" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a href="/review/show/1433414491?book_show_action=true" itemprop="publishDate" class="reviewDate createdAt right">Nov 04, 2015</a>

      <a href="/user/show/31780597-rinu-razak" class="user" title="Rinu Razak">Rinu Razak</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars"><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="liked it">liked it</span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="liked it"></span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="liked it"></span><span class="staticStar p0" size="15x15" title="liked it"></span><span class="staticStar p0" size="15x15" title="liked it"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText"> · </span>
          <a href="/book/show/119382.Sands_of_Time" title="Paperback 9780006174431" class="lightGreyText">review of another edition</a>


        


    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span style="" class="readable" id="reviewTextContainer1433414491">
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2950432569507589863">It's been quite a while since I've been brooding over the desire to read a 'Sidney Sheldon' book. And, Voila! I finally got my hands on his less acclaimed book titled 'Sands of Time'. I was so eager to get to know this famed writer more, that I was excited to read it right away. You could call it a 'book lover's craving' but I should say that I was a bit disappointed in the end. Sheldon is a skilled, accomplished writer who is well-versed in English language, there is no doubt in that but he has</span>
  <span style="display:none" id="freeText2950432569507589863">It's been quite a while since I've been brooding over the desire to read a 'Sidney Sheldon' book. And, Voila! I finally got my hands on his less acclaimed book titled 'Sands of Time'. I was so eager to get to know this famed writer more, that I was excited to read it right away. You could call it a 'book lover's craving' but I should say that I was a bit disappointed in the end. Sheldon is a skilled, accomplished writer who is well-versed in English language, there is no doubt in that but he has tried to describe and visually recreate the lives of so many characters all at once that, eventually towards the end 'the element of spark' I felt at a particular point, was lost. At some point, towards halfway through this fiction, I felt really absorbed but then, the writer spoiled all those build-ups by the time I finished the book.<br />'Sands of Time' is the story which tries to depict the stressful atmosphere and conflicts which existed some years back between the Basque community and the Spanish government. The whole plot revolves around a group of Basque rebels who work under an organization ETA and a group of nuns who were rescued during an army attack at the Cistercian Convent of the Strict Observance just outside Ávila. Jaime Miro, Sister Megan (Patricia), Lucia Carmine, Rubio, Sister Graciela, Ricardo, Sister Teresa, Felix Carpio and Amparo are the central figures in the novel who are chased throughout the story by Colonel Ramón Acoca who is the head of the anti-ETA group named GOE. Several other characters also pop up occasionally, namely Ellen Scott, Alan Tucker and Raoul. Things get interesting to the readers when we reach the crux, but the bliss goes in vain upon winding up the novel. But one thing worth mentioning here is that, I had certain cliched story endings in my mind about 'who goes with whom' but some of those expectations were rewritten by Sheldon diplomatically without letting his readers know about it, unless they dug deep and ponder over the whole plot, in a new perspective. It would be an injustice from my side, if I intentionally ignored this particular aspect of the book.</span>
  <a onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;" href="#" data-text-id="2950432569507589863">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer18195868277059583682">Judul: Bulir-bulir pasir waktu<br />Penulis: Sidney sheldon<br />Penerbit: Sanjaya<br />Dimensi: ebook, 429 hlm, no ISBN<br /><br />Dengan latar Spanyol di tahun 1976, di mana perang saudara--antara kaum Basque yang memperjuangkan kemerdekaannya dengan pemerintah--meletus begitu hebat, penulis mengisahkan suasana saat itu melalui empat tokoh biarawati. Lucia, yang melarikan diri dan menyimpan rahasia pembunuhan yang kejam dari Sisilia. Teresa, wanita alim yang kecewa pada masa lalunya dan memutuskan mengabdi di biara hingga</span>
  <span style="display:none" id="freeText18195868277059583682">Judul: Bulir-bulir pasir waktu<br />Penulis: Sidney sheldon<br />Penerbit: Sanjaya<br />Dimensi: ebook, 429 hlm, no ISBN<br /><br />Dengan latar Spanyol di tahun 1976, di mana perang saudara--antara kaum Basque yang memperjuangkan kemerdekaannya dengan pemerintah--meletus begitu hebat, penulis mengisahkan suasana saat itu melalui empat tokoh biarawati. Lucia, yang melarikan diri dan menyimpan rahasia pembunuhan yang kejam dari Sisilia. Teresa, wanita alim yang kecewa pada masa lalunya dan memutuskan mengabdi di biara hingga 30 tahun. Graciela, wanita cantik dan termuda yang ingin menebus dosa masa lalu saat remaja. Dan Megan, yatim piatu yang memiliki imajinasi serta daya berontak dalam pikirannya. Suatu pagi terpaksa meninggalkan kesucian dan keheningan biara. Melepaskan kehidupan damai dan terpaksa membaurkan diri dalam dunia yang sebenarnya, asing, dan gemerlap. Dunia yang membuat mereka berhadapan dengan nasib tak terduga dan menemukan arti sesungguhnya mengenai eksistensial mereka di dunia.<br /><br />Seperti biasa, Sidney selalu memiliki twist tak terduga. Kali ini mengenai siapa pengkhianat pergerakan kaum Basque. Mengenai detail karakter dan kisah hidup masing-masing tokoh pun dijelaskan dengan rinci dan sesekali menggunakan alur flashback. Tak ada yang luput, hingga semua terasa begitu manusiawi, wajar dengan adanya motif masa lalu, dan tak ada yang salah tergantung dari sudut mana memandangnya. Konflik utama buku ini adalah penangkapan seorang kepala pergerakan bernama Jaime Miro yang dituduh sebagai teroris, oleh Kepala Polisi Accoca. Tak lupa, ada sedikit bumbu konspirasi pergerakan besar tak terlihat yang memainkan perannya, bernama Opus Mundo. Ciri khas lain penulis adalah kisah romantis antara tiap tokohnya dan happy ending.<br /><br />Novel fiksi ini memang hanya terinspirasi oleh sebuah kabar di media, namun terasa bagai nyata. Menggambarkan apa yang terjadi di Spanyol, tentang mimpi dan cita warganya, serta budaya dan sejarah berdarah mereka. Sidney selalu membuat pembacanya betah berlama-lama dengan karyanya, sebab alurnya begitu mengalir, gaya bahasanya ringan dan to the point, dengan kejutan menarik yang sering mematahkan dugaan pembaca. Namun di buku kali ini, kejutannya tidak begitu banyak dan impresif seperti karya sebelumnya yang saya baca.<br /><br />Saya apresiasi 3 dari 5 bintang.<br /><br />"Oh, tetapi Anda tentunya mempunyai banyak teman."<br />"Kenalan. Kalau dipikir benar-benar, siapakah yang benar-benar mempunyai banyak teman?" (Hlm. 149)<br /><br />"Tuhan tidak berpihak, karena Ia ada di dalam diri kita semua. Kita semua adalah suatu bagian dariNya, dan jika kita mencoba menghancurkanNya, maka kita menghancurkan diri kita sendiri." (Hlm. 343)<br /><br />"Tetapi tidak ada jalan pelarian itu, bahkan pada akhirnya, kita semua harus menghadapi yang menjadi tanggung jawab kita masing-masing. Maka aku kembali berpijak di atas bumi ini." (Hlm. 349)<br /><br />Meta morfillah</span>

<div itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope="" itemprop="reviews" class="review nosyndicate" id="review_1421046641">
  <link href="http://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1421046641" itemprop="url" />
  <a href="/user/show/6167794-ana-lukovi" class="left imgcol" title="Ana Lukovi?"><img src="http://d.gr-assets.com/users/1451392392p2/6167794.jpg" alt="Ana Lukovi?" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a href="/review/show/1421046641?book_show_action=true" itemprop="publishDate" class="reviewDate createdAt right">Oct 23, 2015</a>

      <a href="/user/show/6167794-ana-lukovi" class="user" title="Ana Lukovi?">Ana Lukovi?</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars"><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="liked it">liked it</span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="liked it"></span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="liked it"></span><span class="staticStar p0" size="15x15" title="liked it"></span><span class="staticStar p0" size="15x15" title="liked it"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText"> · </span>
          <a href="/book/show/119382.Sands_of_Time" title="Paperback 9780006174431" class="lightGreyText">review of another edition</a>


        


    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span style="" class="readable" id="reviewTextContainer1421046641">
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11281556081277017327">I haven`t read Sheldon in what seems like forever. In reality, it must have been at least two or three years since the last time I read a book of his. What brought me back to his novels was my friend (a Sheldon enthusiast) and the interesting premise. Mostly all of his novels take place in some glamorous, luxurious world filled with heiresses and balls and expensive things beyond imagining. It is an enticing world, but most of us can`t relate to it. It remains an elusive world, one we will proba</span>
  <span style="display:none" id="freeText11281556081277017327">I haven`t read Sheldon in what seems like forever. In reality, it must have been at least two or three years since the last time I read a book of his. What brought me back to his novels was my friend (a Sheldon enthusiast) and the interesting premise. Mostly all of his novels take place in some glamorous, luxurious world filled with heiresses and balls and expensive things beyond imagining. It is an enticing world, but most of us can`t relate to it. It remains an elusive world, one we will probably never know.<br />But, this book promised something completely different. No luxury, no fortunes, no conglomerates (at least, not at the beginning of the story). The protagonists weren`t just ordinary people struggling with ordinary problems – they were nuns! Another aspect of the story that drew me in was the fact that the plot takes place in Spain. And it was clear as to why. In the foreword and the epilogue, Sheldon`s own interest in this country, its people and its history is visible to everyone reading the novel. And who could blame him? While nearly every nation has an interesting and bloody history to a certain degree, the history of Spain can be deemed particularly interesting, especially by history nuts like myself. And the time period Sheldon chose to write about only adds to the suspension of the story.<br />As an action novel, the story works well. It is believable, it is constantly shifting and changing and it has rebellious men fighting for a passionate cause, which adds a dimension of romanticism to the tale. What more could you ask for? An added bonus – four nuns out in the world after a long time, trying to survive under their guidance. Everyone`s got their own sad story of how and why they came to fight for independence or how and why they locked themselves up in a strict convent.<br />The one aspect of the story that just didn`t make sense to me was the love part. I get it – rebels and beautiful women travelling together under constant danger, there are bound to be some sparks flying and some emotions to be stirred. In another world, it might have worked beautifully. But, it was handled so sloppily. All three couples fell in love so suddenly and quickly and without a bit of foundation. One day they`re barely talking to each other and the next one – they`re planning their wedding. Instead of adding to the story, it just felt so forced and unnecessary and it almost ruined the whole thing.<br />There were beautiful parts describing love and loyalty in this novel. But, then again, there were horrible parts concerning war and tyranny. I don`t think I`ll be able to get the image of Teresa`s death out of my head for the next month or so. She was an old lady, driven into insanity by the ghosts of past. There was absolutely no need for such cruelty and the brutal rape she suffered. I felt it was such an unnecessary and brutal scene that never should have been written.<br />Also, even though I couldn`t help but admire Sheldon`s male characters for their passion and loyalty, their cause was lost on me. There is always a point in time when a freedom fighter crosses a line and turns into a common criminal. Maybe I`m just too much of a Pacifist in a world filled with violence, but when put up against life, dignity and pride lose their battle every time. What angered me even more was that they were fighting for their cause diligently and then, one day, they just up and left for France. They created loads of turmoil, but escaped facing it and it just seemed so irresponsible to me.<br />A good read, but not as good as the promising beginning. 2.5 stars.</span>
  <a onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;" href="#" data-text-id="11281556081277017327">...more</a>

          </span>

<div itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope="" itemprop="reviews" class="review" id="review_1468056522">
  <link href="http://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1468056522" itemprop="url" />
  <a href="/user/show/17994985-bobby-underwood" class="left imgcol" title="Bobby Underwood"><img src="http://d.gr-assets.com/users/1442641958p2/17994985.jpg" alt="Bobby Underwood" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a href="/review/show/1468056522?book_show_action=true" itemprop="publishDate" class="reviewDate createdAt right">Jan 04, 2016</a>

      <a href="/user/show/17994985-bobby-underwood" class="user" title="Bobby Underwood">Bobby Underwood</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars"><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="it was amazing">it was amazing</span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="it was amazing"></span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="it was amazing"></span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="it was amazing"></span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="it was amazing"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText"> · </span>
          <a href="/book/show/8881704-the-sands-of-time" title="Hardcover 9781417801930" class="lightGreyText">review of another edition</a>


        


    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span style="" class="readable" id="reviewTextContainer1468056522">
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2449434565875174943">No one wrote a better or more entertaining romantic potboiler than Sidney Sheldon, and The Sands of Time is one of his best. It has loads of color and atmosphere, characters you root for, divergent story-lines each as interesting as the last, and Sheldon's tremendous gift for storytelling, on grand display here. You won't forget Lucia, Teresa, Graciela or Megan, nor will you forget the wonderfully colorful portrait of Spain and its conflicts (though a bit dated) of the time. Like a lot of Sheldo</span>
  <span style="display:none" id="freeText2449434565875174943">No one wrote a better or more entertaining romantic potboiler than Sidney Sheldon, and The Sands of Time is one of his best. It has loads of color and atmosphere, characters you root for, divergent story-lines each as interesting as the last, and Sheldon's tremendous gift for storytelling, on grand display here. You won't forget Lucia, Teresa, Graciela or Megan, nor will you forget the wonderfully colorful portrait of Spain and its conflicts (though a bit dated) of the time. Like a lot of Sheldon's work, it is soapy but not so much so that we lose interest. Anyone who remembers The Other Side of Midnight knows how much fun it can be to read the master of melodrama (or watch, as that book was made into a mini-series for television way back when). For sheer entertainment, you can't beat The Sands of Time. If you've got a few days at the beach, well worth taking with you.</span>
  <a onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;" href="#" data-text-id="2449434565875174943">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer15121483214013726406">This is one of Sidney Sheldon's best books. But not one of the paramount thriller novels of all time. Keen Sheldon fans (like myself) will love it, but the average suspense reader might barely like it.<br /><br />The plot is Sheldon-esque. And the sights of Spain are scenically detailed. Yet, the story becomes easy to foretell after the second half. <br /><br />The Sands of Time is also intriguing for those who are interested in the Spanish Civil War's history - as Sheldon did a tactful job of including bountiful resea</span>
  <span style="display:none" id="freeText15121483214013726406">This is one of Sidney Sheldon's best books. But not one of the paramount thriller novels of all time. Keen Sheldon fans (like myself) will love it, but the average suspense reader might barely like it.<br /><br />The plot is Sheldon-esque. And the sights of Spain are scenically detailed. Yet, the story becomes easy to foretell after the second half. <br /><br />The Sands of Time is also intriguing for those who are interested in the Spanish Civil War's history - as Sheldon did a tactful job of including bountiful research on this proposition.<br /><br />Finally, no part of the narrative is tedious, and that's what matters most in good, old-fashioned storytelling. </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer14877118453273511360">Despite some flaws and fantasy, I enjoyed the book through to the end more than 'Nothing lasts forever' but still I am giving it 4 stars because I think it had too much drama, too many plots and too many 'seriously? can this happen in real?' moments whereas 'Nothing lasts forever' was more realistic.   <span style="display:none" id="freeText14877118453273511360">Despite some flaws and fantasy, I enjoyed the book through to the end more than 'Nothing lasts forever' but still I am giving it 4 stars because I think it had too much drama, too many plots and too many 'seriously? can this happen in real?' moments whereas 'Nothing lasts forever' was more realistic. The story is unique though. <br /><br />It is the story of 4 nuns from different countries with different background that led them to become nuns and by fate; they all end up in one convent. <br /><br />Sister Lucia: A murderer, who came to convent to escape from police. She is the most adventurous one.<br /><br />Sister Megan: Most intelligent one. She ended up in the convent after her parents were killed in plane crash.<br /><br />Sister Graciela: She is the most beautiful one. She falls in love with a terrorist but will she marry him? <br /><br />Sister Teresa: She is the oldest one. She became nun to run away from the man who betrayed her. <br /><br />One day, their convent gets raided by armies and while these 4 nuns try to escape, they unexpectedly get encountered with terrorists. This encounter changes their lives and now they are struggling to choose a way they should live their lives. Where will they go? Will they go back to where they came from? <br /><br />Watch out for Sidney Sheldon. He has a reputation for making his readers bookworms. <br /><br />Published on: <a rel="nofollow" href="http://pchhantyal.blogspot.de/2014/08/sands-of-time-by-sidney-sheldon.html" target="_blank">http://pchhantyal.blogspot.de/2014/08...</a></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span style="" class="readable" id="reviewTextContainer730098273">
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9075087578719650766">Spain - a land of eternal passion and unceasing bloodshed. Fleeing the vengeance of a pitiless tyrant, four nuns find themselves suddenly thrust into a hostile world which they had long ago abandoned for the safety of the convent. Unwittingly, they become pawns in a battle between the charismatic Jaime Miró, leader of the outlawed Basque nationalists, and the ruthless Colonel Ramón Acoca of the Spanish Army.<br /><br />Lucia - the fiery Sicilian beauty who harbors a murderous secret; she wins the heart of R</span>
  <span style="display:none" id="freeText9075087578719650766">Spain - a land of eternal passion and unceasing bloodshed. Fleeing the vengeance of a pitiless tyrant, four nuns find themselves suddenly thrust into a hostile world which they had long ago abandoned for the safety of the convent. Unwittingly, they become pawns in a battle between the charismatic Jaime Miró, leader of the outlawed Basque nationalists, and the ruthless Colonel Ramón Acoca of the Spanish Army.<br /><br />Lucia - the fiery Sicilian beauty who harbors a murderous secret; she wins the heart of Rubio Arzano, a freedom fighter who risks his life to save her.<br /><br />Graciella - whose guilt over one reckless, youthful sin continues to haunt her, even now; Ricardo is the courageous man who loves her.<br /><br />Megan - the orphan seeking perilous refuge in the arms of a defiant Basque rebel; Jaime Miró, himself.<br /><br />Teresa - the believer haunted by a faith that seemingly mocks her with silence; whose own guilty conscience may lead her to commit an unforgivable act.<br /><br />Four women - and the men they are forbidden to love. Leaving innocence but not hope behind, they venture into an alien, dazzling world, where each will encounter an unexpected destiny - and the truth about herself. <br /><br />I really enjoyed this book. It was a quick read for me, and learning about the pasts of each of the women was certainly intriguing. I give this book a definite A!</span>
  <a onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;" href="#" data-text-id="9075087578719650766">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

            Shelves:
              <a href="/review/list/10382635-ginny-1807?shelf=non-fa-per-me" class="actionLinkLite">non-fa-per-me</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span style="" class="readable" id="reviewTextContainer409114618">
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16326254747551405339">Fecondo confezionatore di bestsellers americani tipici degli anni Settanta/Ottanta – caratterizzati da trame tortuose altamente improbabili e inframmezzati da urticanti descrizioni esplicite di sesso – Sidney Sheldon ha prodotto romanzi di un certo interesse come “L’altra faccia di mezzanotte” che, pur nei limiti del genere commercial-popolare a cui è da ascrivere, presentava uno sviluppo abbastanza convincente delle vicende e una fascinosa caratterizzazione dei personaggi. Romanzi da scegliere</span>
  <span style="display:none" id="freeText16326254747551405339">Fecondo confezionatore di bestsellers americani tipici degli anni Settanta/Ottanta – caratterizzati da trame tortuose altamente improbabili e inframmezzati da urticanti descrizioni esplicite di sesso – Sidney Sheldon ha prodotto romanzi di un certo interesse come “L’altra faccia di mezzanotte” che, pur nei limiti del genere commercial-popolare a cui è da ascrivere, presentava uno sviluppo abbastanza convincente delle vicende e una fascinosa caratterizzazione dei personaggi. Romanzi da scegliere e da fruire come letture passatempo scacciapensieri, insomma; ma tali da non offendere il buonsenso e l’intelligenza dei lettori. <br />“Le sabbie del tempo”, al contrario, si rivela una solenne presa in giro, in quanto tratta temi impegnativi come la questione basca o le problematiche connesse alle vocazioni e alla regola degli ordini religiosi con una superficialità ed approssimazione addirittura irritanti. <br />In particolare il finale, improntato al più scontato e deteriore romanticismo da telenovela-spazzatura, denuncia un vergognoso asservimento dello scrittore alle richieste di un mercato di infima categoria e di discutibile spessore ideologico. <br />In conclusione: uno dei libri più insulsi che abbia mai letto.</span>

<div itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope="" itemprop="reviews" class="review" id="review_8547330">
  <link href="http://www.goodreads.com/review/show/8547330" itemprop="url" />
  <a href="/user/show/443960-trouble" class="left imgcol" title="Trouble"><img src="http://d.gr-assets.com/users/1191593076p2/443960.jpg" alt="Trouble" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a href="/review/show/8547330?book_show_action=true" itemprop="publishDate" class="reviewDate createdAt right">Nov 01, 2007</a>

      <a href="/user/show/443960-trouble" class="user" title="Trouble">Trouble</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars"><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="liked it">liked it</span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="liked it"></span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="liked it"></span><span class="staticStar p0" size="15x15" title="liked it"></span><span class="staticStar p0" size="15x15" title="liked it"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText"> · </span>
          <a href="/book/show/119382.Sands_of_Time" title="Paperback 9780006174431" class="lightGreyText">review of another edition</a>

          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">people who like romance novels</span></div>

        


    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span style="" class="readable" id="reviewTextContainer8547330">
            
<span id="freeTextContainer817358334725992034">Recommended to me by a Japanese person studying English, she described Sheldon as an author who was popular in the 70s...which makes sense, since I couldn`t read in the 70s and I`ve never heard of the person before.<br /><br />With no expectations, I gave the book a try - and it didn`t disappoint, though without expectations, this isn`t too much of a feat. It reads like a romance novel with slightly more substance.<br /><br />The plot centers around a group of nuns during the Revolution in Spain - three are actually nu</span>
  <span style="display:none" id="freeText817358334725992034">Recommended to me by a Japanese person studying English, she described Sheldon as an author who was popular in the 70s...which makes sense, since I couldn`t read in the 70s and I`ve never heard of the person before.<br /><br />With no expectations, I gave the book a try - and it didn`t disappoint, though without expectations, this isn`t too much of a feat. It reads like a romance novel with slightly more substance.<br /><br />The plot centers around a group of nuns during the Revolution in Spain - three are actually nuns, one is masquerading in the convent to hide from the police. The convent these ladies are living in is attacked by police for supposedly harboring a political activist; the four escape with the convent`s prize treasure: a large, ornate gold cross. <br /><br />Three out of the four, having lived cloistered for the past ten-twenty-fourty years, are completely helpless out in the wild world, while the Bad Nun plots to steal the cross and run away with the fortune. Then, of course, they are intercepted by the political activist and his merry band of terrorists, and everyone falls in love, gets married, and lives happily ever after.<br /><br />Well, not quite. The twists sometimes seem like the author is deliberately trying to avoid being cliche - there is the bad-girl-going-good, the orphaned-rich-heiress, the-guilt-stricken-good-girl and so on, so it`s a bit like having four romance novels mashed together. Not all their endings are the ones you`d find on the supermarket rack though, so if you`re looking for something light and fluffy with two cups of sex and a generous spoonful of history, all tied up with a convenient bow at the end, this may be worth checking out.<br /><br />I wouldn`t spend money on it unless it particularly resonates with you - make a library trip for it, it`s not a long or difficult read.</span>
  <a onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;" href="#" data-text-id="817358334725992034">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked &amp;&amp; exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&amp;name=' + shelf_name + '&amp;a=' + action + '&amp;authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('JOth5kKswaUtCU0/CoccTkCR+BiGVXkCLjDGBxDBhvlBP141sH7VX6HROYR05vr8CWY7Ac+IPqhEOcOV3FRwvA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&amp;book_id=' + book_id + '&amp;refresh=true' + '&amp;authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('O+fuiMCYJ5pKi+OpaFMjr18qsPlMy4MvQ2F7HLjhka5eM9FbMkozYMZTlxIWMsUdFt1z4AUWxIUpaH6OdHRn6w==')})
  }

    <div class=" clearFloats bigBox" id="aboutAuthor"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/author/show/9068.Sidney_Sheldon">About Sidney Sheldon</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
      <a href="/author/show/9068.Sidney_Sheldon"><img alt="9068" src="http://d.gr-assets.com/authors/1209169297p2/9068.jpg" class="right" /></a>
    <div class="readable">
      
<span id="freeTextContainer17158089628932817602">Was an American writer who won awards in three careers—a Broadway playwright, a Hollywood TV and movie screenwriter, and a best-selling novelist. His TV works spanned a 20-year period during which he created I Dream of Jeannie (1965-70), Hart to Hart (1979-84), and The Patty Duke Show (1963-66), but it was not until after he turned 50 and began writing best-selling novels such as Master of the Gam</span>
  <span style="display:none" id="freeText17158089628932817602">Was an American writer who won awards in three careers—a Broadway playwright, a Hollywood TV and movie screenwriter, and a best-selling novelist. His TV works spanned a 20-year period during which he created I Dream of Jeannie (1965-70), Hart to Hart (1979-84), and The Patty Duke Show (1963-66), but it was not until after he turned 50 and began writing best-selling novels such as Master of the Game (1982), The Other Side of Midnight (1973) and Rage of Angels (1980) that he became most famous.</span>
  <a onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;" href="#" data-text-id="17158089628932817602">...more</a>

    </div>
